These generated files are configured in CODEOWNERS to be owned by @grafanabot. The system also generates feature toggle documentation (docs/sources/setup-grafana/configure-grafana/feature-toggles/index.md) from the registry definitions.\\n\\nTypeScript integration occurs through packages/grafana-data/src/types/featureToggles.gen.ts (generated TypeScript types) and scripts/cli/generateBettererIssues.ts, which uses the npm codeowners library to parse the CODEOWNERS file and map code quality issues to team owners. The package.json declares the codeowners dependency (version ^5.1.1) and includes npm scripts like \\\"betterer:issues\\\" that leverage this parsing.\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API layer (pkg/apis/featuretoggle/v0alpha1/types.go) defines the FeatureSpec type with an Owner field (JSON field name 'codeowner'), enabling feature toggle ownership to be exposed through the API. The corresponding OpenAPI schema (zz_generated.openapi.go) documents this field. The contribute/feature-toggles.md guide documents the workflow for adding new feature toggles, instructing developers to set the Owner property for all feature flags and use the CODEOWNERS file conventions.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
